class=\"content-ad-block navigation-not-searchable\"><div id=\"rocketleague_336x280_BTF\"></div></div></div></div>\n<div class=\"fo-nttax-infobox-wrapper\"><div class=\"fo-nttax-infobox wiki-bordercolor-light\"><div><div class=\"infobox-header wiki-backgroundcolor-light\">Upcoming Matches</div></div></div></div>\n<p><b>RLCS 2021-22</b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2021, crossing over into 2022. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with more regions and an updated format. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each have 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collects points that will determine whether they will qualify for the World Championship or World Championship Wildcard.\n</p>\n<div id=\"toc\" class=\"toc\" class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class=\"thumb tright\"><div class=\"thumbinner\" style=\"width:337px;\"><a href=\"/rocketleague/File:Swiss_System_Graphic.png\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"/commons/images/thumb/e/e7/Swiss_System_Graphic.png/335px-Swiss_System_Graphic.png\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"335\" height=\"712\" class=\"thumbimage\" 5\">Bo5</abbr>.</li></ul></li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(221,244,221);\">Top 8</span> Teams proceed to the <a America/2\">Playoffs</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<p><br />\n</p>\n<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>October 30th - 31st, 2021</i>\n<ul><li>Single Elimination Bracket.\n<ul><li>All matches are a <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> except the Grand Finals, which are a <abbr title=\"Best of 3\">Bo3</abbr> set for a <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> (First to win 2 <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr> series).</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Prize_Pool\">Prize Pool</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span
